getRandomInt(max) {\n            return Math.floor(Math.random() * Math.floor(max));\n        }\n\n        function between(x, min, max) {\n          return x >= min && x <= max;\n        }\n\n        function duplicateEmojis() {\n            $(\'.emoji\').each(function() {\n                $(this).clone().appendTo($(".emojis"));\n            });\n        }\n\n        function randomizeEmojis() {\n            $(\'.emoji\').each(function() {\n                var randomScale = parseFloat(getRandomInt(10) + 5) / 10 ;\n                $(this).find("svg").css({\'transform\': \'scale(\' + randomScale + \')\'});\n                var randomTop, randomLeft;\n                while(!randomTop || !between(randomTop, 10, 30) && !between(randomTop, 70, 90)) {\n                    randomTop = getRandomInt(100);\n                }\n                while(!randomLeft || !between(randomLeft, 10, 30) && !between(randomLeft, 70, 90)) {\n                    randomLeft = getRandomInt(100);\n                }\n                $(this).css({\'top\': randomTop + \'%\', \'left\': randomLeft + \'%\'});\n            });\n        }\n\n        duplicateEmojis();\n        randomizeEmojis();\n        window.setTimeout(function() {\n            randomizeEmojis();\n            window.setInterval(function() {\n                randomizeEmojis();\n            }, 8000);\n        }, 4000);\n    });\n</script>\n    </section>\n\n    <section id="home-instagram" class="container-fluid pt-4 pt-lg-5 pb-5 px-0">\n        \n\n\n\n    <div class="container-fluid px-4">\n        <div class="row
